create table OE_ORDER_HEADERS_ALL
   (	"HEADER_ID" NUMBER , 
	"ORDER_NUMBER" NUMBER, 
	"CUST_PO_NUMBER" VARCHAR2(50 BYTE), 
	"ORDERED_DATE" DATE, 
	"FLOW_STATUS_CODE" VARCHAR2(30 BYTE), 
	"CREATION_DATE" DATE, 
	"LAST_UPDATE_DATE" DATE, 
	"ATTRIBUTE11" VARCHAR2(240 BYTE), 
	"ATTRIBUTE12" VARCHAR2(240 BYTE), 
	"ATTRIBUTE13" VARCHAR2(240 BYTE), 
	"ORDER_CATEGORY_CODE" VARCHAR2(30 BYTE), 
	"SHIP_LOCATION" VARCHAR2(40 BYTE), 
	"SHIP_NAME" VARCHAR2(240 BYTE), 
	"BILL_LOCATION" VARCHAR2(40 BYTE), 
	"BILL_NAME" VARCHAR2(240 BYTE)
   )

select ah.sold_to_org_id -- hz_cust_accounts
,ah.SHIP_TO_ORG_ID -- hz_cust_site_uses_all.site_use_id
,ah.INVOICE_TO_ORG_ID -- hz_cust_site_uses_all.site_use_id
,ah.HEADER_ID
,ah.ORDER_NUMBER
,ah.CUST_PO_NUMBER
,ah.ORDERED_DATE
,ah.FLOW_STATUS_CODE
,ah.CREATION_DATE
,ah.LAST_UPDATE_date
,ah.attribute11
,ah.attribute12
,ah.attribute13
,ah.order_category_code 
,hz_csua_ship.location
,ps_ship.PARTY_SITE_NAME
,hz_csua_bill.location
,ps_bill.PARTY_SITE_NAME
from 
oe_order_headers_all ah,
hz_cust_acct_sites_all hz_casa_ship,
hz_cust_site_uses_all hz_csua_ship,
hz_party_sites ps_ship,
hz_cust_acct_sites_all hz_casa_bill,
hz_cust_site_uses_all hz_csua_bill,
hz_party_sites ps_bill
where cust_po_number = '3038-9021826ATD02'
  and hz_csua_ship.cust_acct_site_id = hz_casa_ship.cust_acct_site_id
  and hz_csua_ship.site_use_id =ah.SHIP_TO_ORG_ID
  and ps_ship.party_site_id = hz_casa_ship.party_site_id 
    and hz_csua_bill.cust_acct_site_id = hz_casa_bill.cust_acct_site_id
  and hz_csua_bill.site_use_id =ah.INVOICE_TO_ORG_ID
  and ps_bill.party_site_id = hz_casa_bill.party_site_id
